 agar modi he to ye 200 pratishat hona chahie

 piem modi ne kaha ki ek shaayar ne kaha tha ki:use gumaan he ki meri udaan kuch kam hamujhe yaqin he ki ye aasmaan kuch kam he

 us par ateet kaa boj nahin hota, aise main chunautiyon or samasyaon se nipatane main wo adhik sakasham hota he
 The number of deer killed in Delhi's zoo (national Zoological Park) is being reported up to 36
 ju prashasan ne rebies kii vajah se 17 hiranon ke marane kii pushti kii he
 The Zoo administration has immediately sought help from the National Center for Disease Control (NCDC) due to the death of deer
 NCDC se madad kii apiladarasal ju athurity kii ore se 18 may ko ek khateenchhichhko likhaa gaya he, jisamen chidyaghar main rebies ke badhate prakope kaa zikr kiya gaya he
 According to the Zoo Authority, the risk of rabies is now hitting on the people working in the zoo
 halaat kaabo hone ke bajaay dinon-din bigadataa ja rahaa he
 According to the Xu administration, all measures are taken to control the diseases spread in the domestic animals, which are available there, but the situation is not improving
 jiske baad ab ju prashasan madad ko lekar NCDC ko khat likhaa he
 According to Jariju authority, the sewer water of Delhi Jal Board entered the deer enclosure on 14 February 2016
 jiske baad gande pani ko to hataa diya gaya lekin usase baad achaanak tinhiranon kii mautaho gai
 The post-mortem report revealed that the deer drank the dirty water of that sewer
 ju prashasan ne maut kii vajah jaanane ke liye mrit hiranon ke sample ko jaanch ke liye bhartiya pashu chikitsa anusandhan santhaan (iviarai) bheja
 Investigations revealed that the deer died of rabies
 jiske baad se chidyaghar main dusron jaanwaron kii lagaataar jaanch kii ja rahi he ki kahin is rebies kii chapet main wo na aa jaaen
 Ju administration is also accused of negligence, although questions are being raised about the death of deer administration
 ju prashasan par shuruyaat main hi maamle ko gambhirtha se nahin lene kaa aarope he
 Also, there is a charge of increasing the death toll of deer due to negligence
 ab jab halaat behad gambhir ho gaye hai to ju prashasan sakriy hua he
